msg:I came to the nearby area for a business trip on the weekend. There are not many hotels with four diamonds or above. I finally chose Binjiang New Century Grand. Overall, the experience is good. Here are the specific performances:
Facilities: The hotel has more advantages than disadvantages, so I will start with the disadvantages. I hope the hotel can improve in the future. 1. There is a problem with the air conditioner switch in the room I stayed in. After turning on the air conditioner and adjusting it to 20 degrees for 2 hours, the indoor temperature rose from 25 degrees when I just entered the room to 26 degrees. Later, I turned off the air conditioner and opened the window to feel a little more comfortable; 2. Closing the door next door will cause resonance of the door in my room, which affects my rest, and the voices in the corridor will be clearly transmitted to the room. The sound insulation of the door is poor; 3. The room is a non-smoking room, but there is always a more obvious smell of smoke. Because there are many things to do, I did not ask to change rooms. I hope the hotel can check this point; 4. I personally suggest that screens can be installed on the windows to prevent mosquitoes. Advantages: 1. The TV is larger than that of ordinary hotels, and the viewing effect is good; 2. The takeaway is delivered to the door by a robot, which is fast; 3. The room and toilet are large, the overall decoration is avant-garde, and the stay experience is good; 4. The breakfast has a wide variety and tastes good. It is one of the few delicious breakfasts in Hangzhou. Recommended.
Hygiene: Overall, it is okay. The toilet, bed, and sofa are relatively clean and there are no obvious stains.
Environment: As one of the few high-rise buildings around, the scenery is still good. See the picture for reference.
Service: The handling experience is very good. The lady at the front desk No. 12 handled it quickly, explained patiently and in detail, and upgraded the room for me. Good comments
